\Hypertarget{group__I2S__Register__Masks_gad21e3586a7f3600aa25a1e186a8e9eb9}\index{I2S Register Masks@{I2S Register Masks}!I2S\_MCR\_DUF@{I2S\_MCR\_DUF}}
\index{I2S\_MCR\_DUF@{I2S\_MCR\_DUF}!I2S Register Masks@{I2S Register Masks}}
\doxysubsubsubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{I2S\_MCR\_DUF}{I2S\_MCR\_DUF}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__I2S__Register__Masks_gad21e3586a7f3600aa25a1e186a8e9eb9} 
\+\#define I2\+S\+\_\+\+MCR\+\_\+\+DUF(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

{\bfseries Value:\+}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{(((uint32\_t)(((uint32\_t)(x))\ <<\ I2S\_MCR\_DUF\_SHIFT))\ \&\ I2S\_MCR\_DUF\_MASK)}

\end{DoxyCode}
DUF -\/ Divider Update Flag 0b0..MCLK divider ratio is not being updated currently. 0b1..MCLK divider ratio is updating on-\/the-\/fly. Further updates to the MCLK divider ratio are blocked while this flag remains set.
